The rainbow flag is a beloved and universally-recognized symbol of #Pride and support for the #LGBTQ+ community across the world! üè≥Ô∏è‚Äçüåà(6/6)
a brown and a black stripe to the top to represent LGBTQ+ people of color (the black stripe is also sometimes added to represent those lost to the AIDS epidemic). (5/6)
began to be mass-produced in 1979 following the assassination of Harvey Milk, the pink and turquoise stripes were dropped for logistical reasons. We have been using the six-striped version ever since! In 2017, the city of Philadelphia created a new version that added (4/6)
had eight stripes instead of the current six, adding a pink stripe and a turquoise stripe. The colors each had a meaning assigned to it: pink=sex, red=life, orange=healing, yellow=sunlight, green=nature, turquoise=magic/art, blue=serenity, and purple=spirit. When the flag (3/6)
